                    <h3 class="post-title entry-title">
                     <a href="http://www.productreviewscanada.com/2015/04/african-american-culture-and-news.html">
                      African-American Culture and News
                     </a>
                    </h3>
                    <div class="post-header">
                     <div class="post-header-line-1">
                      <div class="post-share-buttons goog-inline-block">
                       <a class="goog-inline-block share-button sb-email" href="https://www.blogger.com/share-post.g?blogID=801925266976884095&amp;postID=5363690521583835923&amp;target=email" target="_blank" title="Email This">

                       <a class="goog-inline-block share-button sb-pinterest" href="https://www.blogger.com/share-post.g?blogID=801925266976884095&amp;postID=5363690521583835923&amp;target=pinterest" target="_blank" title="Share to Pinterest">

                        <g:plusone annotation="inline" href="http://www.productreviewscanada.com/2015/04/african-american-culture-and-news.html" size="medium" source="blogger:blog:plusone" width="300">

                      <span class="post-timestamp">

                    <div class="post-body entry-content" id="post-body-5363690521583835923">
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-tMv1jvO0ypU/VR2U65wGOyI/AAAAAAAAfwU/dtN54J8vgOU/s1600/Barack%2BObama%2BWashington.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="clear: right; float: right; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 1em;">
                       <img border="0" height="211" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-tMv1jvO0ypU/VR2U65wGOyI/AAAAAAAAfwU/dtN54J8vgOU/s1600/Barack%2BObama%2BWashington.jpg" width="320"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     Appreciating African-American Culture And Entertainment
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     African-American culture isn't entirely different from some mainstream 
cultures, but it's different enough that African-Americans feel an 
emptiness when they look at mainstream media. They don't see people who 
look, think, and talk like them, and they detect a noticeable absence of
 African-American figures in the arenas of politics and business. For 
those people who want their children to grow up appreciating their 
culture, and for those African-Americans who want to hold onto their own
 culture, there are channels that broadcast
                     <a href="http://www.eurweb.com/category/eurweb-exclusives/" target="_blank">
                      African American news and issues
                     </a>
                     that hit home with its audience.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     News and issues
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     News and issues focus on central figures in the African-American 
community that are up and coming on the political scene or that are 
doing noteworthy things in the community. There are also stories of 
community news that deal with noteworthy legal issues that might be 
pressing for the African-American community.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     Sports and entertainment
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     It's not all serious on African-American channels. There are 
entertainment and sports features that bring home those genres to the 
masses and give the entertainment an African-American voice to 
appreciate. This might include musicians, actors, sports figures, and 
stand-up artists who bring joy to the world through those gifts.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     You don't have to be African-American to appreciate the culture. Anyone 
can tune in, just like African-Americans also watch mainstream networks 
and news shows that focus on a more causation audience. Diversity in our
 entertainment broadens horizons across the board for people across 
cultures.
                     <div style="clear: both;">
                     </div>
                    </div>

                    <h3 class="post-title entry-title">
                     <a href="http://www.productreviewscanada.com/2015/01/james-bond-vs-spectre.html">
                      James Bond Vs Spectre
                     </a>
                    </h3>
                    <div class="post-header">
                     <div class="post-header-line-1">
                      <div class="post-share-buttons goog-inline-block">
                       <a class="goog-inline-block share-button sb-email" href="https://www.blogger.com/share-post.g?blogID=801925266976884095&amp;postID=7345693591453517451&amp;target=email" target="_blank" title="Email This">

                       <a class="goog-inline-block share-button sb-pinterest" href="https://www.blogger.com/share-post.g?blogID=801925266976884095&amp;postID=7345693591453517451&amp;target=pinterest" target="_blank" title="Share to Pinterest">

                       <div class="goog-inline-block dummy-container">
                        <g:plusone annotation="inline" href="http://www.productreviewscanada.com/2015/01/james-bond-vs-spectre.html" size="medium" source="blogger:blog:plusone" width="300">

                      </div>
                      <span class="post-timestamp">
                       at
                       <a class="timestamp-link" href="http://www.productreviewscanada.com/2015/01/james-bond-vs-spectre.html" rel="bookmark" title="permanent link">

                    <div class="post-body entry-content" id="post-body-7345693591453517451">
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-QrcMPih5Q80/VLQ9mXzxYYI/AAAAAAAAeso/PQuW1Jtj5mE/s1600/Spectre%2BMovie%2BPoster.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="clear: right; float: right; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 1em;">
                       <img border="0" height="640" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-QrcMPih5Q80/VLQ9mXzxYYI/AAAAAAAAeso/PQuW1Jtj5mE/s1600/Spectre%2BMovie%2BPoster.jpg" width="432"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     So it was announced recently that the new James Bond film, starring Daniel Craig, will be called "
                     <b>
                      Spectre
                     </b>
                     ".
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     And if you are like many Canadians, you can name most of the James Bond films, you have a favourite actor who played James Bond (mine is Roger Moore, but Daniel Craig is pretty awesome too), and you probably can't wait to see the new 007 film, which is due to be released on
                     <b>
                      November 6th 2015
                     </b>
                     .
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     So the good news is that Spectre is back - a villainous organization dating back to a time when that hack Sean Connery was playing James Bond (seriously, Connery just says his lines and looks good, he doesn't have any acting skill).
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     You know what I would really love however?
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     <b>
                      Jaws.
                     </b>
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     Bring back Jaws, the villain-turned-hero who appeared in two different James Bond films and becomes a hero by the end of the 2nd film. I know who would be a good actor to play Jaws as well - the guy who played
                     <span class="irc_su" dir="ltr" style="text-align: left;">
                      Ser Gregor Clegane or The Mountain That Rides" in Game of Thrones, also known as
                     </span>
                     <b>
                      Hafthor Bjornsson
                     </b>
                     . The guy is so big he makes Arnold look small, which makes him a great option to play Jaws.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     At 6'9" tall, 386 lbs Hafthor Bjornsson can not only play Jaws, but as one of the top 5 strongest men currently alive - and the only one of those who is an actor, he can play the role well. The guy dresses up as the Incredible Hulk just for fun.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     But in the meantime, just for fun, lets have a look at the introductory music videos found at the start of the last 3 James Bond films made by Daniel Craig.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     <center>
                      CASINO ROYALE
                      <br/>
                      <iframe allowfullscreen="" frameborder="0" height="315" src="//www.youtube.com/embed/Kg5lI6NCBxE" width="560">
                      </iframe>
                      <br/>
                      <br/>
                      <br/>
                      QUANTUM OF SOLACE
                      <br/>
                      <iframe allowfullscreen="" frameborder="0" height="315" src="//www.youtube.com/embed/YMXT3aJxH_A" width="560">
                      </iframe>
                      <br/>
                      <br/>
                      <br/>
                      SKYFALL
                      <br/>
                      <iframe allowfullscreen="" frameborder="0" height="315" src="//www.youtube.com/embed/_4gdhsVKTcs" width="560">
                      </iframe>
                      <br/>
                      <br/>
                     </center>

                    <h3 class="post-title entry-title">
                     <a href="http://www.productreviewscanada.com/2015/01/free-trial-of-mega-flix.html">
                      Free Trial of Mega Flix
                     </a>
                    </h3>
                    <div class="post-header">
                     <div class="post-header-line-1">
                      <div class="post-share-buttons goog-inline-block">
                       <a class="goog-inline-block share-button sb-email" href="https://www.blogger.com/share-post.g?blogID=801925266976884095&amp;postID=6400717525663488678&amp;target=email" target="_blank" title="Email This">
                        <span class="share-button-link-text">
                         Email This
                        </span>
                       </a>
                       <a class="goog-inline-block share-button sb-blog" href="https://www.blogger.com/share-post.g?blogID=801925266976884095&amp;postID=6400717525663488678&amp;target=blog" onclick='window.open(this.href, "_blank", "height=270,width=475"); return false;' target="_blank" title="BlogThis!">
                        <span class="share-button-link-text">
                         BlogThis!
                        </span>
                       </a>
                       <a class="goog-inline-block share-button sb-twitter" href="https://www.blogger.com/share-post.g?blogID=801925266976884095&amp;postID=6400717525663488678&amp;target=twitter" target="_blank" title="Share to Twitter">
                        <span class="share-button-link-text">
                         Share to Twitter
                        </span>
                       </a>
                       <a class="goog-inline-block share-button sb-facebook" href="https://www.blogger.com/share-post.g?blogID=801925266976884095&amp;postID=6400717525663488678&amp;target=facebook" onclick='window.open(this.href, "_blank", "height=430,width=640"); return false;' target="_blank" title="Share to Facebook">
                        <span class="share-button-link-text">
                         Share to Facebook
                        </span>
                       </a>
                       <a class="goog-inline-block share-button sb-pinterest" href="https://www.blogger.com/share-post.g?blogID=801925266976884095&amp;postID=6400717525663488678&amp;target=pinterest" target="_blank" title="Share to Pinterest">
                        <span class="share-button-link-text">
                         Share to Pinterest
                        </span>
                       </a>
                       <div class="goog-inline-block dummy-container">
                        <g:plusone annotation="inline" href="http://www.productreviewscanada.com/2015/01/free-trial-of-mega-flix.html" size="medium" source="blogger:blog:plusone" width="300">
                        </g:plusone>
                       </div>
                      </div>
                      <span class="post-timestamp">
                       at
                       <a class="timestamp-link" href="http://www.productreviewscanada.com/2015/01/free-trial-of-mega-flix.html" rel="bookmark" title="permanent link">
                        <abbr class="published" title="2015-01-07T18:02:00-08:00">
                         6:02 PM
                        </abbr>
                       </a>
                      </span>
                     </div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="post-body entry-content" id="post-body-6400717525663488678">
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-Vvki4d7UKhQ/VK3k9GVx3HI/AAAAAAAAekQ/vYXMniJAgsI/s1600/Netflix%2BLogo.png" imageanchor="1" style="clear: right; float: right; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 1em;">
                       <img border="0" height="180" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-Vvki4d7UKhQ/VK3k9GVx3HI/AAAAAAAAekQ/vYXMniJAgsI/s1600/Netflix%2BLogo.png" width="320"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     Watching movies online for free is just one of those things many people do these days. Especially if you are into downloading your films for free.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     However having the convenience of watching movies sooner - and not having to wait for the film to download - is rather nice to have. This is why I have a subscription to Netflix.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     But there are other companies which offer movie downloading - including free trials.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     For example:
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     <a href="http://offertracking.linkvehicle.com/aff_c?offer_id=246&amp;aff_id=3268" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                      Mega Flix has a 5 Day Free Trial
                     </a>
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-OcXomiYiDqg/VK3k2eeLHtI/AAAAAAAAekI/qm2k1DViHkM/s1600/CraveTV%2BLogo.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="clear: right; float: right; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 1em;">
                       <img border="0" height="180" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-OcXomiYiDqg/VK3k2eeLHtI/AAAAAAAAekI/qm2k1DViHkM/s1600/CraveTV%2BLogo.jpg" width="320"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     Recently I have also been thinking of getting CraveTV ( see http://www.cravetv.ca/ ) just for the convenience of being able to watch as much TV shows as I want for only $4 per month. That is just ridiculously cheap and good value.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     CraveTV has Game of Thrones, Dallas, Sopranos, Seinfeld, Big Bang Theory, Corner Gas, Monty Python (the TV show and all the films) and a whole lot more. It is very tempting. However there is just one flaw:
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     Most of the shows on there that I would want, I already own on DVD. Or have access to on Netflix.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     So at this point I am undecided. That doesn't mean however that CraveTV might not be right for you. Maybe you don't have Netflix like I do. Or maybe you prefer to download everything for free (in which case, check out that free trial - it is basically 5 days worth of free movies).
                     <div style="clear: both;">
                     </div>
                    </div>

                    <h3 class="post-title entry-title">
                     <a href="http://www.productreviewscanada.com/2014/12/the-interview-5-stars.html">
                      THE INTERVIEW - 5 STARS
                     </a>
                    </h3>
                    <div class="post-header">
                     <div class="post-header-line-1">
                      <div class="post-share-buttons goog-inline-block">
                       <a class="goog-inline-block share-button sb-email" href="https://www.blogger.com/share-post.g?blogID=801925266976884095&amp;postID=968531458639106480&amp;target=email" target="_blank" title="Email This">
                        <span class="share-button-link-text">
                         Email This
                        </span>
                       </a>
                       <a class="goog-inline-block share-button sb-blog" href="https://www.blogger.com/share-post.g?blogID=801925266976884095&amp;postID=968531458639106480&amp;target=blog" onclick='window.open(this.href, "_blank", "height=270,width=475"); return false;' target="_blank" title="BlogThis!">
                        <span class="share-button-link-text">
                         BlogThis!
                        </span>
                       </a>
                       <a class="goog-inline-block share-button sb-twitter" href="https://www.blogger.com/share-post.g?blogID=801925266976884095&amp;postID=968531458639106480&amp;target=twitter" target="_blank" title="Share to Twitter">

                         Share to Twitter
                        </span>
                       </a>
                       <a class="goog-inline-block share-button sb-facebook" href="https://www.blogger.com/share-post.g?blogID=801925266976884095&amp;postID=968531458639106480&amp;target=facebook" onclick='window.open(this.href, "_blank", "height=430,width=640"); return false;' target="_blank" title="Share to Facebook">

                       <a class="goog-inline-block share-button sb-pinterest" href="https://www.blogger.com/share-post.g?blogID=801925266976884095&amp;postID=968531458639106480&amp;target=pinterest" target="_blank" title="Share to Pinterest">

                        </span>
                       </a>
                       <div class="goog-inline-block dummy-container">
                        <g:plusone annotation="inline" href="http://www.productreviewscanada.com/2014/12/the-interview-5-stars.html" size="medium" source="blogger:blog:plusone" width="300">
                        </g:plusone>
                       </div>
                      </div>
                      <span class="post-timestamp">
                       at
                       <a class="timestamp-link" href="http://www.productreviewscanada.com/2014/12/the-interview-5-stars.html" rel="bookmark" title="permanent link">
                        <abbr class="published" title="2014-12-29T10:01:00-08:00">
                         10:01 AM
                        </abbr>
                       </a>

                    <div class="post-body entry-content" id="post-body-968531458639106480">
                     Review by Charles Moffat - December 2014.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     <div style="text-align: center;">
                      <span style="font-size: large;">
                       <i>
                        "The best comedy of the year."
                       </i>
                      </span>
                     </div>
                     <br/>
                     Note - "The Interview" starring Seth Rogen and James Franco was
                     <b>
                      Made in Canada
                     </b>
                     - which means, arguably, that North Korea should be threatening Canada, not the USA for its production.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-_os65eAfFtQ/VKGVIUb3AII/AAAAAAAAeQs/XFdX2B7mGqk/s1600/The%2BInterview%2B2014%2Bmovie%2Bposter.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="clear: right; float: right; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 1em;">
                       <img border="0" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-_os65eAfFtQ/VKGVIUb3AII/AAAAAAAAeQs/XFdX2B7mGqk/s1600/The%2BInterview%2B2014%2Bmovie%2Bposter.jpg"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     I have been wanting to see this film for months, ever since I heard about it. Partially because I used to live in South Korea, but also because I want to see an end to the war between the USA and North Korea - which has been in a state of cold war for 61 years now. The Korean War may have ended in 1953, but the war never officially ended because they never signed an armistice. This means that for 61 years North Korea has been in a state of war with the USA and South Korea, and there has been numerous skirmishes between north and south, but it hasn't been a case of active war.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     In recent years North Korea has been ramping up its long range missile development and its focus on nuclear weapons. The country currently has the capability of launching ICBM nuclear missiles across the Pacific Ocean and striking targets in the western USA, Hawaii and Alaska.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     And to make matters worse, the leadership of North Korea has been handing from father to son, so the current leader of North Korea is a 31 year old man. A man which has been tasked with defeating the USA, staying in power while his people starve, and smashing any hopes of rebellion against him.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     Thus making a comedy about two American reporters sent to kill him is just hilarious with the premise alone, but I want to make clear here that having watched the film myself that this film is extremely well scripted, well written, and well acted. The best comedy of the year, in my opinion.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     Thus I am giving it FIVE STARS out of five.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     And I am not just saying this just because I have an interest in North Korea's eventual defeat and reunification with South Korea, I sincerely believe this film is the best comedy film I have seen this year.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     <center>
                      <iframe allowfullscreen="" frameborder="0" height="309" src="//www.youtube.com/embed/Ed2kSuKqfz0" width="550">
                      </iframe>
                      <br/>
                     </center>
                     <br/>
                     When North Korea heard about the comedy they became worried about what it might contain that would embarrass their country and their "supreme leader", and you know what, the film does not disappoint. The film brilliantly shows off Kim Jong-un as a maniacal dictator who pretends to be a god.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     Sony, which funded the film ended up pulling the movie out of movie theatres due to terrorist death threats made against audiences that watched it, but later released it on YouTube anyway (for a fee) and also released it to privately owned art theatres.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     Thus the film won't make as much money as originally predicted, but it is my opinion that this film should be seen by millions of people anyway - simply because it is that good.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     Case in point - My girlfriend doesn't like the actor Seth Rogen, but she ended up liking the film anyway. Kind of like how I like Romeo and Juliet, even though I cannot stand Leonardo DiCaprio.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     *
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     *
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     *
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     SPOILER ALERT
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     There are many parts of the film I really enjoyed, but my favourite part is when Kim Jong-un cries so hard that he s**** himself.
                     <div style="clear: both;">
                     </div>
                    </div>

                    <h3 class="post-title entry-title">
                     <a href="http://www.productreviewscanada.com/2014/08/my-search-for-old-archery-movies.html">
                      My Search for Old Archery Movies
                     </a>
                    </h3>
                    <div class="post-header">
                     <div class="post-header-line-1">
                      <div class="post-share-buttons goog-inline-block">
                       <a class="goog-inline-block share-button sb-email" href="https://www.blogger.com/share-post.g?blogID=801925266976884095&amp;postID=8957577134548032088&amp;target=email" target="_blank" title="Email This">
                        <span class="share-button-link-text">
                         Email This
                        </span>
                       </a>
                       <a class="goog-inline-block share-button sb-blog" href="https://www.blogger.com/share-post.g?blogID=801925266976884095&amp;postID=8957577134548032088&amp;target=blog" onclick='window.open(this.href, "_blank", "height=270,width=475"); return false;' target="_blank" title="BlogThis!">
                        <span class="share-button-link-text">
                         BlogThis!
                        </span>
                       </a>
                       <a class="goog-inline-block share-button sb-twitter" href="https://www.blogger.com/share-post.g?blogID=801925266976884095&amp;postID=8957577134548032088&amp;target=twitter" target="_blank" title="Share to Twitter">
                        <span class="share-button-link-text">
                         Share to Twitter
                        </span>
                       </a>
                       <a class="goog-inline-block share-button sb-facebook" href="https://www.blogger.com/share-post.g?blogID=801925266976884095&amp;postID=8957577134548032088&amp;target=facebook" onclick='window.open(this.href, "_blank", "height=430,width=640"); return false;' target="_blank" title="Share to Facebook">
                        <span class="share-button-link-text">
                         Share to Facebook
                        </span>
                       </a>
                       <a class="goog-inline-block share-button sb-pinterest" href="https://www.blogger.com/share-post.g?blogID=801925266976884095&amp;postID=8957577134548032088&amp;target=pinterest" target="_blank" title="Share to Pinterest">
                        <span class="share-button-link-text">
                         Share to Pinterest
                        </span>
                       </a>
                       <div class="goog-inline-block dummy-container">
                        <g:plusone annotation="inline" href="http://www.productreviewscanada.com/2014/08/my-search-for-old-archery-movies.html" size="medium" source="blogger:blog:plusone" width="300">
                        </g:plusone>
                       </div>
                      </div>
                      <span class="post-timestamp">
                       at
                       <a class="timestamp-link" href="http://www.productreviewscanada.com/2014/08/my-search-for-old-archery-movies.html" rel="bookmark" title="permanent link">
                        <abbr class="published" title="2014-08-20T06:37:00-07:00">
                         6:37 AM
                        </abbr>
                       </a>
                      </span>
                     </div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="post-body entry-content" id="post-body-8957577134548032088">
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/--RSCvUPwA7c/U_SPbrIhxZI/AAAAAAAAcWk/z0dNrLrlFZM/s1600/Elvis%2BTeaching%2BArchery.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="clear: right; float: right; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 1em;">
                       <img border="0" height="320" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/--RSCvUPwA7c/U_SPbrIhxZI/AAAAAAAAcWk/z0dNrLrlFZM/s1600/Elvis%2BTeaching%2BArchery.jpg" width="285"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     Lately for fun I have been researching and browsing old movies that have archery in them. Sometimes even just brief archery clips in the films.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     For example the photo on the right is a movie still from the Elvis movie "
                     <b>
                      Tickle Me
                     </b>
                     ", during which Elvis briefly teaches an archery lesson.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     But much better examples of old archery movies are films like:
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     <b>
                      The Flame and the Arrow
                     </b>
                     - starring Burt Lancaster (who is frankly awesome in everything he does).
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     Or
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     <a href="http://www.productreviewscanada.com/2013/09/a-man-called-horse-movie-review.html" target="_blank">
                      <b>
                       A Man Called Horse
                      </b>
                     </a>
                     - starring Irish actor Richard Harris, whom you may recognize from his many other movies - including playing Dumbledore in the first 2 Harry Potter movies.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     Or
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     <b>
                      Deliverance
                     </b>
                     - starring Burt Reynolds and Jon Voight (I don't care for Voight, but Burt Reynolds is again very awesome. What is it with actors named Burt being so awesome???)
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     Below is the movie trailer for Deliverance.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     <center>
                      <iframe allowfullscreen="" frameborder="0" height="375" src="//www.youtube.com/embed/-3Jr7af1FrQ" width="500">
                      </iframe>
                      <br/>
                     </center>
                     <br/>
                     And of course there is also films like Rambo II, Rambo III and all the various Robin Hood films...
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     Robin Hood - 1938, starring Errol Flynn (with archery stunts by Howard Hill).
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     Robin Hood Prince of Thieves - 1991, starring Kevin Costner.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     Robin Hood - 1973, Disney animated film.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     Those are three of the more famous ones.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     But there is actually many more Robin Hood films...
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     Robin Hood - 2010 with Russell Crowe
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     Robin Hood - 1991 with Patrick Bergin and Uma Thurman
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     Robin and Marian - 1976
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     Robin Hood Men in Tights - 1993
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     The Story of Robin Hood and his Merrie Men - 1952, Disney live action
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     The Men of Sherwood Forest - 1954
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     Rabbit Hood - 1949 with Bugs Bunny
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     Beyond Sherwood Forest - 2009
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     And a slew of other Robin Hood films...
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     During my research I have determined there hasn't been a lot of William Tell movies made (a planned one for 2012 starring Brendan Fraser was scrapped when the producers ran into financial difficulties getting funding for their film).
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     There is an old Austrian William Tell movie from 1960, in German of course. Good luck finding an English dubbed version.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     And an older William Tell film from 1949 - and a 1998 TV series called "The Legend of William Tell" with 15 episodes (which looks gawd awful, like a cheap rip off of Xena Warrior Princess).
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     During my research I have determined there was a lot of archery films (especially Robin Hood or Robin Hood esque films) made during the 1940s and 1950s. It was part of an archery fad that started with enormous financial success of the Errol Flynn / Howard Hill film in 1938, and the fad continued until the early 1970s and included the 1972 film
                     <b>
                      Deliverance
                     </b>
                     starring Burt Reynolds.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     There was a brief renewed interest in archery in the 1980s when 2nd and 3rd
                     <b>
                      Rambo
                     </b>
                     movies came out, and again in 1991 with
                     <b>
                      Robin Hood Prince of Thieves
                     </b>
                     - but it was nothing like the fad from 1940s to 1970s.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     With the introduction of the Lord of the Rings trilogy in 2001 archery saw a bit of interest, but the fast shooting abilities of Legolas made archery look beyond the skill of the common man.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     A couple years later however something interesting happened.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     Alabama, at that point the fattest state in the USA, was trying to come to grips with an obesity epidemic and high schools were looking for ways to get teenagers outside and exercising. So someone came up with the idea of starting an archery club in one of the schools. The club took off in popularity, the model was spread to other schools in Alabama, and eventually the program was expanded to other states.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     By the time films like the
                     <b>
                      Hunger Games, Brave, The Avengers, Killing Season, Hanna
                     </b>
                     and other archery films came out archery was already a growing phenomenon in the USA.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     And when those films became popular it was partially because archery was growing as a fad. It was the fad fueling the films, not the other way around. (Although at this point it is more cyclical, archery fanatics are fueling the films and the films are creating new archery fanatics.)
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     Below is the movie trailer for
                     <b>
                      Killing Season
                     </b>
                     , starring Robert De Niro and John Travolta.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     <center>
                      <iframe allowfullscreen="" frameborder="0" height="281" src="//www.youtube.com/embed/_yseYEtQoJQ" width="500">
                      </iframe>
                      <br/>
                     </center>

                     </div>

                     <a href="http://www.productreviewscanada.com/2014/08/expendables-3-movie-review.html">
                      Expendables 3 - Movie Review
                     </a>
                    </h3>
                    <div class="post-header">
                     <div class="post-header-line-1">
                      <div class="post-share-buttons goog-inline-block">
                       <a class="goog-inline-block share-button sb-email" href="https://www.blogger.com/share-post.g?blogID=801925266976884095&amp;postID=7058294507907430580&amp;target=email" target="_blank" title="Email This">

                       </a>

                       <a class="goog-inline-block share-button sb-twitter" href="https://www.blogger.com/share-post.g?blogID=801925266976884095&amp;postID=7058294507907430580&amp;target=twitter" target="_blank" title="Share to Twitter">

                      </div>
                      <span class="post-timestamp">
                       at
                       <a class="timestamp-link" href="http://www.productreviewscanada.com/2014/08/expendables-3-movie-review.html" rel="bookmark" title="permanent link">

                    <div class="post-body entry-content" id="post-body-7058294507907430580">
                     So if you enjoyed Expendables 1 and Expendables 2, then you will probably enjoy Expendables 3.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     I give it 3.5 stars out of 5. A friend of mine gives it 3 stars.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     Why? Because it was good, it was entertaining, but it wasn't spectacular.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     The highlight of the movie was Antonio Banderas stealing the show.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-kUBnm_gEZZo/U_IaHEZ9L2I/AAAAAAAAcV0/P3AYsiuZpW4/s1600/Expendables%2B3%2BPoster.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                       <img border="0" height="292" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-kUBnm_gEZZo/U_IaHEZ9L2I/AAAAAAAAcV0/P3AYsiuZpW4/s1600/Expendables%2B3%2BPoster.jpg" width="640"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     <br/>
                     <br/>

                    <div class="post-body entry-content" id="post-body-8370580741236603534">

                    <h3 class="post-title entry-title">
                     <a href="http://www.productreviewscanada.com/2014/08/into-storm-movie-review-night-of.html">
                      Into The Storm, movie review + "Night of the Twisters"
                     </a>
                    </h3>
                    <div class="post-header">
                     <div class="post-header-line-1">
                      <div class="post-share-buttons goog-inline-block">
                       <a class="goog-inline-block share-button sb-email" href="https://www.blogger.com/share-post.g?blogID=801925266976884095&amp;postID=7726637985123710478&amp;target=email" target="_blank" title="Email This">
                        <span class="share-button-link-text">
                         Email This
                        </span>
                       </a>
                       <a class="goog-inline-block share-button sb-blog" href="https://www.blogger.com/share-post.g?blogID=801925266976884095&amp;postID=7726637985123710478&amp;target=blog" onclick='window.open(this.href, "_blank", "height=270,width=475"); return false;' target="_blank" title="BlogThis!">

                       <a class="goog-inline-block share-button sb-twitter" href="https://www.blogger.com/share-post.g?blogID=801925266976884095&amp;postID=7726637985123710478&amp;target=twitter" target="_blank" title="Share to Twitter">
                        <span class="share-button-link-text">

                        </span>

                       <a class="goog-inline-block share-button sb-facebook" href="https://www.blogger.com/share-post.g?blogID=801925266976884095&amp;postID=7726637985123710478&amp;target=facebook" onclick='window.open(this.href, "_blank", "height=430,width=640"); return false;' target="_blank" title="Share to Facebook">

                        </span>
                       </a>
                       <a class="goog-inline-block share-button sb-pinterest" href="https://www.blogger.com/share-post.g?blogID=801925266976884095&amp;postID=7726637985123710478&amp;target=pinterest" target="_blank" title="Share to Pinterest">
                        <span class="share-button-link-text">
                         Share to Pinterest
                        </span>
                       </a>
                       <div class="goog-inline-block dummy-container">
                        <g:plusone annotation="inline" href="http://www.productreviewscanada.com/2014/08/into-storm-movie-review-night-of.html" size="medium" source="blogger:blog:plusone" width="300">
                        </g:plusone>
                       </div>
                      </div>
                      <span class="post-timestamp">
                       at
                       <a class="timestamp-link" href="http://www.productreviewscanada.com/2014/08/into-storm-movie-review-night-of.html" rel="bookmark" title="permanent link">
                        <abbr class="published" title="2014-08-14T05:40:00-07:00">
                         5:40 AM
                        </abbr>
                       </a>
                      </span>
                     </div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="post-body entry-content" id="post-body-7726637985123710478">
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-3RvOcfNAgqw/U-ytRObJSTI/AAAAAAAAcTM/4NArSk65hbQ/s1600/Into%2BThe%2BStorm%2BPoster.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="clear: right; float: right; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 1em;">
                       <img border="0" height="250" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-3RvOcfNAgqw/U-ytRObJSTI/AAAAAAAAcTM/4NArSk65hbQ/s1600/Into%2BThe%2BStorm%2BPoster.jpg" width="400"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     So the remake of "
                     <b>
                      Night of the Twisters
                     </b>
                     " came out recently, with a name change and some plot changes - but it is essentially the same movie.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     Don't believe me? Watch "
                     <b>
                      Into The Storm
                     </b>
                     " at the movie theatre and then watch "Night of the Twisters" on YouTube further below.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     The biggest difference between the two movies is that "Into The Storm" has infinitely better graphics. Behind the tornadoes, the drama in both movies is an emphasis on the importance of family and perseverance/survival.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     I give the graphics for Into The Storm 5 stars - but I only give the drama / plot 3 stars. Honestly, I would watch tornado movies just for the graphics if the movie was nothing but tornadoes and just skip the plot entirely. Just 2 hours of mind-blowing graphics and tornado carnage would be something I would love to watch.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     <center>
                      INTO THE STORM, TRAILER
                      <br/>
                      <br/>
                      <iframe allowfullscreen="" frameborder="0" height="281" src="//www.youtube.com/embed/57Vkp77tVTM" width="500">
                      </iframe>
                      <br/>
                      <br/>
                      NIGHT OF THE TWISTERS, FULL MOVIE
                      <br/>
                      <br/>
                      <iframe allowfullscreen="" frameborder="0" height="375" src="//www.youtube.com/embed/T9zOQUkU7iI" width="500">
                      </iframe>
                      <br/>
                     </center>

                    <div class="post-body entry-content" id="post-body-2966012913783772127">
                     Saw this movie poster further below recently when I went to see the new Hercules movie (starring Dwayne "The Rock" Johnson as Hercules) which was "good / okay", but nothing spectacular. I liked the fact that they made the Hercules story more realistic - no magic or gods whatsoever in the film - and how it played upon the myth vs reality theme.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     BTW, watch the credits at the end of Hercules - totally worth it.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     Anyway, back to the Mockingjay poster... Is it just me or does the Mockingjay look a bit like the Toronto Blue Jays' logo? True, they're both jays, but the similarities feel like they go beyond that. Copyright infringement, probably not. Especially when you look at the Blue Jays pumpkin further below.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">

                       <img border="0" height="640" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-kMl0S061Kv8/U9qTx8X8WII/AAAAAAAAcEA/xgKfVCb5fuY/s1600/Mockingjay+Part+1+Poster.jpg" width="480"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>

                    <h3 class="post-title entry-title">
                     <a href="http://www.productreviewscanada.com/2014/02/youtubes-random-movies-go-up-and-later.html">
                      YouTubes Random Movies go up and later come down
                     </a>
                    </h3>
                    <div class="post-header">
                     <div class="post-header-line-1">
                      <div class="post-share-buttons goog-inline-block">
                       <a class="goog-inline-block share-button sb-email" href="https://www.blogger.com/share-post.g?blogID=801925266976884095&amp;postID=6494332153182842719&amp;target=email" target="_blank" title="Email This">
                        <span class="share-button-link-text">
                         Email This
                        </span>
                       </a>
                       <a class="goog-inline-block share-button sb-blog" href="https://www.blogger.com/share-post.g?blogID=801925266976884095&amp;postID=6494332153182842719&amp;target=blog" onclick='window.open(this.href, "_blank", "height=270,width=475"); return false;' target="_blank" title="BlogThis!">
                        <span class="share-button-link-text">
                         BlogThis!
                        </span>
                       </a>
                       <a class="goog-inline-block share-button sb-twitter" href="https://www.blogger.com/share-post.g?blogID=801925266976884095&amp;postID=6494332153182842719&amp;target=twitter" target="_blank" title="Share to Twitter">
                        <span class="share-button-link-text">
                         Share to Twitter
                        </span>
                       </a>
                       <a class="goog-inline-block share-button sb-facebook" href="https://www.blogger.com/share-post.g?blogID=801925266976884095&amp;postID=6494332153182842719&amp;target=facebook" onclick='window.open(this.href, "_blank", "height=430,width=640"); return false;' target="_blank" title="Share to Facebook">
                        <span class="share-button-link-text">
                         Share to Facebook
                        </span>
                       </a>
                       <a class="goog-inline-block share-button sb-pinterest" href="https://www.blogger.com/share-post.g?blogID=801925266976884095&amp;postID=6494332153182842719&amp;target=pinterest" target="_blank" title="Share to Pinterest">
                        <span class="share-button-link-text">
                         Share to Pinterest
                        </span>
                       </a>
                       <div class="goog-inline-block dummy-container">
                        <g:plusone annotation="inline" href="http://www.productreviewscanada.com/2014/02/youtubes-random-movies-go-up-and-later.html" size="medium" source="blogger:blog:plusone" width="300">
                        </g:plusone>
                       </div>
                      </div>
                      <span class="post-timestamp">
                       at
                       <a class="timestamp-link" href="http://www.productreviewscanada.com/2014/02/youtubes-random-movies-go-up-and-later.html" rel="bookmark" title="permanent link">
                        <abbr class="published" title="2014-02-15T12:59:00-08:00">
                         12:59 PM
                        </abbr>
                       </a>
                      </span>
                     </div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="post-body entry-content" id="post-body-6494332153182842719">
                     If you search for the term "full movie" on YouTube you can find a variety of free movies (many of them Bollywood or Asian movies) that you can watch in HD without having to pay a cent.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     Two days ago I watched "White House Down" (the 2013 action film) in HD thanks to some random person who uploaded it. (The film itself was good, I give it 4.5 stars out of 5. I even had tears in my eyes at the end when
                     <span style="color: red;">
                      *SPOILER ALERT*
                     </span>
                     the daughter waved the American flag on the White House lawn.)
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     Today the movie is gone. Deleted by YouTube's 'copyright infringement police'.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-PVGnHh_CUrk/Uv_RhkXT-MI/AAAAAAAAZ5g/N7a8Rd6Bs6E/s1600/White-House-Down-YouTube.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                       <img border="0" height="359" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-PVGnHh_CUrk/Uv_RhkXT-MI/AAAAAAAAZ5g/N7a8Rd6Bs6E/s1600/White-House-Down-YouTube.jpg" width="640"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     <br/>
                     But call it the beauty of YouTube, the copyright infringement police only pay attention to popular movies that came out recently - and what is more they only seem to care if the film is English.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     If you browse the long list of films on there (many of them in HD) you will notice that older films and foreign films are widely abundant and all free. Because if it is not new or not in English, then YouTube doesn't care about copyright infringement.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     So huzzah. If you're bored and want to watch a random movie for free, just go to YouTube, type full movie in the search and pick from recent releases (which will soon be deleted), old movies (which they don't care about), or foreign films (which might even be recent).
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     You could watch for example:
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     <center>
                      Sky Riders, an American action film released in 1976.
                      <br/>
                      <br/>
                      <iframe allowfullscreen="" frameborder="0" height="309" src="//www.youtube.com/embed/-f0O5AAxDtM?rel=0" width="550">
                      </iframe>
                      <br/>
                      <br/>
                      Or you could watch
                      <br/>
                      <br/>
                      The Defender, a Chinese action film starring Jet Li released in 2013
                      <br/>
                      <br/>
                      <iframe allowfullscreen="" frameborder="0" height="309" src="//www.youtube.com/embed/a-3D6bcrjUM?rel=0" width="550">
                      </iframe>
                      <br/>
                      <br/>
                      Not to be confused with...
                      <br/>
                      <br/>
                      The Defender, the 2004 movie starring Dolph Lundgren
                      <br/>
                      <br/>
                      <iframe allowfullscreen="" frameborder="0" height="413" src="//www.youtube.com/embed/qf5iCB5CmJY?rel=0" width="550">
                      </iframe>
                      <br/>
                     </center>
                     <br/>
                     Silliness. :)

                    </a>
                    <h3 class="post-title entry-title">
                     <a href="http://www.productreviewscanada.com/2014/02/the-crown-and-dragon.html">
                      The Crown and the Dragon
                     </a>
                    </h3>
                    <div class="post-header">
                     <div class="post-header-line-1">
                      <div class="post-share-buttons goog-inline-block">
                       <a class="goog-inline-block share-button sb-email" href="https://www.blogger.com/share-post.g?blogID=801925266976884095&amp;postID=2735377329673535856&amp;target=email" target="_blank" title="Email This">
                        <span class="share-button-link-text">
                         Email This
                        </span>
                       </a>
                       <a class="goog-inline-block share-button sb-blog" href="https://www.blogger.com/share-post.g?blogID=801925266976884095&amp;postID=2735377329673535856&amp;target=blog" onclick='window.open(this.href, "_blank", "height=270,width=475"); return false;' target="_blank" title="BlogThis!">
                        <span class="share-button-link-text">
                         BlogThis!
                        </span>
                       </a>
                       <a class="goog-inline-block share-button sb-twitter" href="https://www.blogger.com/share-post.g?blogID=801925266976884095&amp;postID=2735377329673535856&amp;target=twitter" target="_blank" title="Share to Twitter">
                        <span class="share-button-link-text">
                         Share to Twitter
                        </span>
                       </a>
                       <a class="goog-inline-block share-button sb-facebook" href="https://www.blogger.com/share-post.g?blogID=801925266976884095&amp;postID=2735377329673535856&amp;target=facebook" onclick='window.open(this.href, "_blank", "height=430,width=640"); return false;' target="_blank" title="Share to Facebook">
                        <span class="share-button-link-text">
                         Share to Facebook
                        </span>
                       </a>
                       <a class="goog-inline-block share-button sb-pinterest" href="https://www.blogger.com/share-post.g?blogID=801925266976884095&amp;postID=2735377329673535856&amp;target=pinterest" target="_blank" title="Share to Pinterest">
                        <span class="share-button-link-text">
                         Share to Pinterest
                        </span>
                       </a>
                       <div class="goog-inline-block dummy-container">
                        <g:plusone annotation="inline" href="http://www.productreviewscanada.com/2014/02/the-crown-and-dragon.html" size="medium" source="blogger:blog:plusone" width="300">
                        </g:plusone>
                       </div>
                      </div>
                      <span class="post-timestamp">
                       at
                       <a class="timestamp-link" href="http://www.productreviewscanada.com/2014/02/the-crown-and-dragon.html" rel="bookmark" title="permanent link">
                        <abbr class="published" title="2014-02-13T19:51:00-08:00">
                         7:51 PM
                        </abbr>
                       </a>
                      </span>
                     </div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="post-body entry-content" id="post-body-2735377329673535856">
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-J_mhFXIZ3r4/UwPENIBanlI/AAAAAAAAaCM/IfNgRbO7xx0/s1600/The+Crown+and+the+Dragon.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                       <img border="0" height="320" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-J_mhFXIZ3r4/UwPENIBanlI/AAAAAAAAaCM/IfNgRbO7xx0/s1600/The+Crown+and+the+Dragon.jpg" width="640"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     <br/>
                     The Crown and the Dragon is a low budget fantasy movie - but with a fairly good plot, considering its a low budget film.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     <center>
                      <iframe allowfullscreen="" frameborder="0" height="309" src="//www.youtube.com/embed/6g5RTS72QLo?rel=0" width="550">
                      </iframe>
                      <br/>
                     </center>
                     <br/>
                     There are a lot of cheesy low budget fantasy films out there - and many of them are outright horrible. But I must admit the writers put in some extra effort when they were making "The Crown and the Dragon".
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     I think this extra narrative quality comes from the fact the movie is based off a book from the book series "The Paladin Cycle", as opposed to most low budget films which are based on a horribly written script. Movies based off of successful books are always going to be more successful.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     Take for example the low budget movie "Orc Wars" - which is based on a horribly written script. You can tell the difference between the two films easily just from the quality of the narrative. "The Crown and the Dragon" also had a better budget - nothing spectacular, but enough to make better looking dragons and costumes - whereas in "Orc Wars" some of the orcs are wearing jeans and boots with shoelaces... which shows the costume designers for "Orc Wars" just plain didn't care and had a really small budget to work with.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     <center>
                      <iframe allowfullscreen="" frameborder="0" height="309" src="//www.youtube.com/embed/ZrjUCOn9GoA?rel=0" width="550">
                      </iframe>
                      <br/>
                     </center>
                     <div style="clear: both;">
                     </div>
                    </div>

                 <h2 class="date-header">
                  <span>
                   Friday, January 3, 2014
                  </span>
                 </h2>
                 <div class="date-posts">
                  <div class="post-outer">
                   <div class="post hentry">
                    <a name="1531621829522642624">
                    </a>
                    <h3 class="post-title entry-title">
                     <a href="http://www.productreviewscanada.com/2014/01/frank-baum-magical-stories.html">
                      Frank Baum's Magical Stories
                     </a>
                    </h3>
                    <div class="post-header">
                     <div class="post-header-line-1">
                      <div class="post-share-buttons goog-inline-block">
                       <a class="goog-inline-block share-button sb-email" href="https://www.blogger.com/share-post.g?blogID=801925266976884095&amp;postID=1531621829522642624&amp;target=email" target="_blank" title="Email This">
                        <span class="share-button-link-text">
                         Email This
                        </span>
                       </a>
                       <a class="goog-inline-block share-button sb-blog" href="https://www.blogger.com/share-post.g?blogID=801925266976884095&amp;postID=1531621829522642624&amp;target=blog" onclick='window.open(this.href, "_blank", "height=270,width=475"); return false;' target="_blank" title="BlogThis!">
                        <span class="share-button-link-text">
                         BlogThis!
                        </span>
                       </a>
                       <a class="goog-inline-block share-button sb-twitter" href="https://www.blogger.com/share-post.g?blogID=801925266976884095&amp;postID=1531621829522642624&amp;target=twitter" target="_blank" title="Share to Twitter">
                        <span class="share-button-link-text">
                         Share to Twitter
                        </span>
                       </a>
                       <a class="goog-inline-block share-button sb-facebook" href="https://www.blogger.com/share-post.g?blogID=801925266976884095&amp;postID=1531621829522642624&amp;target=facebook" onclick='window.open(this.href, "_blank", "height=430,width=640"); return false;' target="_blank" title="Share to Facebook">
                        <span class="share-button-link-text">
                         Share to Facebook
                        </span>
                       </a>
                       <a class="goog-inline-block share-button sb-pinterest" href="https://www.blogger.com/share-post.g?blogID=801925266976884095&amp;postID=1531621829522642624&amp;target=pinterest" target="_blank" title="Share to Pinterest">
                        <span class="share-button-link-text">
                         Share to Pinterest
                        </span>
                       </a>
                       <div class="goog-inline-block dummy-container">
                        <g:plusone annotation="inline" href="http://www.productreviewscanada.com/2014/01/frank-baum-magical-stories.html" size="medium" source="blogger:blog:plusone" width="300">
                        </g:plusone>
                       </div>
                      </div>
                      <span class="post-timestamp">
                       at
                       <a class="timestamp-link" href="http://www.productreviewscanada.com/2014/01/frank-baum-magical-stories.html" rel="bookmark" title="permanent link">
                        <abbr class="published" title="2014-01-03T17:10:00-08:00">
                         5:10 PM
                        </abbr>
                       </a>
                      </span>
                     </div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="post-body entry-content" id="post-body-1531621829522642624">
                     <div>
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div>
                      Written by Tamyka Bullen
                     </div>
                     <div>
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div>
                      Recently, I started collecting Frank Baum's classical books about the adventurous world of OZ. Probably, his works were just the seeds for next generation writers to bring more fantasy and magics in novels in the Christianized countries. Christianity doesn't allow any magics as they believe that they are the practices of the devil. When the Wizard of OZ movie was on the T.V; my blood rushed, I took the seat excitedly before it had started. When the movie started, my eyes fixed on the rich and colourful world full of fascinating creatures such as Tin Man, Lion King, Scarecrow man, flying monkeys, Munchkins, Witches, and the fake Wizard! Because at my time, closed caption for Deaf people didn't exist. I was fascinated with magics because all my life, witchcraft was my number one obsession. Years later, the Disney company decided to sell the DVDs of the movie, I rushed to the HMV and bought it.
                     </div>
                     <div>
                      Yay yay yay...OZ: The Great and Powerful movie came out on the theatre. I was like WHAT!!! I WANT TO WATCH IT. I waited until the DVDs were on the shelves in any stores, I bought it and watched it right away. The movie was so good. I started to develop my admiration for the Green Witch. Eventually, I bought the Wizard of OZ monopoly game from the bookstore and the LIFE magazine featured fully on the Wizard of OZ. I have all Frank's books of the Wonderland of OZ. In the future, I will buy my favourite characters, Dorothy and Wicked Witch of the West!
                     </div>
                     <div>
                      Here are the pictures of my collection so far!
                     </div>
                     <div>
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div>
                      <div class="separator" style="clear: both;">
                       <a href="https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/-vrhfreVCc2U/UsjEwR13dqI/AAAAAAAAAGU/RRHIoFB3Kzk/s640/blogger-image-1184244273.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                        <img border="0" src="https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/-vrhfreVCc2U/UsjEwR13dqI/AAAAAAAAAGU/RRHIoFB3Kzk/s640/blogger-image-1184244273.jpg"/>
                       </a>
                      </div>
                      <div class="separator" style="clear: both;">
                       Frank Baum wrote fifteen stories about the OZ.
                      </div>
                      <div class="separator" style="clear: both;">
                       <br/>
                      </div>
                      <div class="separator" style="clear: both;">
                       <br/>
                      </div>
                      <div class="separator" style="clear: both;">
                       <a href="https://lh4.googleusercontent.com/-9zpjyMy0n3c/UsjEuPaPBdI/AAAAAAAAAGM/63S5_AVxNlk/s640/blogger-image-1018769959.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                        <img border="0" src="https://lh4.googleusercontent.com/-9zpjyMy0n3c/UsjEuPaPBdI/AAAAAAAAAGM/63S5_AVxNlk/s640/blogger-image-1018769959.jpg"/>
                       </a>
                      </div>
                      <div class="separator" style="clear: both;">
                       I bought this magazine a few months ago because the movie is still the number one favourite for 75 years!
                      </div>
                      <div class="separator" style="clear: both;">
                       <br/>
                      </div>
                      <div class="separator" style="clear: both;">
                       <br/>
                      </div>
                      <div class="separator" style="clear: both;">
                       <a href="https://lh3.googleusercontent.com/-PbRHZnYOmrI/UsjEyJROJ_I/AAAAAAAAAGc/8eZoNWr79Kk/s640/blogger-image-1578696709.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                        <img border="0" src="https://lh3.googleusercontent.com/-PbRHZnYOmrI/UsjEyJROJ_I/AAAAAAAAAGc/8eZoNWr79Kk/s640/blogger-image-1578696709.jpg"/>
                       </a>
                      </div>
                      <div class="separator" style="clear: both;">
                       I used to play the Monopoly game with my family when I was a kid. When the bookstore was selling this game with the Wizard of OZ features, I was like I MUST HAVE IT! So I have it! Lalala lalala
                      </div>
                      <div class="separator" style="clear: both;">
                       <br/>
                      </div>

                    </a>
                    <h3 class="post-title entry-title">
                     <a href="http://www.productreviewscanada.com/2014/01/tom-jones-foundling-bbc-mini-series.html">
                      Tom Jones - A Foundling, the BBC Mini Series
                     </a>
                    </h3>
                    <div class="post-header">
                     <div class="post-header-line-1">
                      <div class="post-share-buttons goog-inline-block">
                       <a class="goog-inline-block share-button sb-email" href="https://www.blogger.com/share-post.g?blogID=801925266976884095&amp;postID=5711833854024901642&amp;target=email" target="_blank" title="Email This">
                        <span class="share-button-link-text">
                         Email This
                        </span>
                       </a>
                       <a class="goog-inline-block share-button sb-blog" href="https://www.blogger.com/share-post.g?blogID=801925266976884095&amp;postID=5711833854024901642&amp;target=blog" onclick='window.open(this.href, "_blank", "height=270,width=475"); return false;' target="_blank" title="BlogThis!">
                        <span class="share-button-link-text">
                         BlogThis!
                        </span>
                       </a>
                       <a class="goog-inline-block share-button sb-twitter" href="https://www.blogger.com/share-post.g?blogID=801925266976884095&amp;postID=5711833854024901642&amp;target=twitter" target="_blank" title="Share to Twitter">
                        <span class="share-button-link-text">
                         Share to Twitter
                        </span>
                       </a>
                       <a class="goog-inline-block share-button sb-facebook" href="https://www.blogger.com/share-post.g?blogID=801925266976884095&amp;postID=5711833854024901642&amp;target=facebook" onclick='window.open(this.href, "_blank", "height=430,width=640"); return false;' target="_blank" title="Share to Facebook">
                        <span class="share-button-link-text">
                         Share to Facebook
                        </span>
                       </a>
                       <a class="goog-inline-block share-button sb-pinterest" href="https://www.blogger.com/share-post.g?blogID=801925266976884095&amp;postID=5711833854024901642&amp;target=pinterest" target="_blank" title="Share to Pinterest">
                        <span class="share-button-link-text">
                         Share to Pinterest
                        </span>
                       </a>
                       <div class="goog-inline-block dummy-container">
                        <g:plusone annotation="inline" href="http://www.productreviewscanada.com/2014/01/tom-jones-foundling-bbc-mini-series.html" size="medium" source="blogger:blog:plusone" width="300">
                        </g:plusone>
                       </div>
                      </div>
                      <span class="post-timestamp">
                       at
                       <a class="timestamp-link" href="http://www.productreviewscanada.com/2014/01/tom-jones-foundling-bbc-mini-series.html" rel="bookmark" title="permanent link">
                        <abbr class="published" title="2014-01-02T20:00:00-08:00">
                         8:00 PM
                        </abbr>
                       </a>
                      </span>
                     </div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="post-body entry-content" id="post-body-5711833854024901642">
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-15kg07xFV_4/UsY0UQCVUcI/AAAAAAAAYU8/2f6gKcRNwoo/s1600/Tom+Jones+A+Foundling.png" imageanchor="1" style="clear: right; float: right; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 1em;">
                       <img border="0" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-15kg07xFV_4/UsY0UQCVUcI/AAAAAAAAYU8/2f6gKcRNwoo/s1600/Tom+Jones+A+Foundling.png"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     One of my favourite mini series of all time is a BBC production of "Tom Jones - A Foundling", which tells the story of an orphan boy adopted by a wealthy nobleman...
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     And the chaos that ensues as the rascally boy comes to age.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     Written by Henry Fielding and first published in 1749 it has nothing to do with the singer "Tom Jones", who is himself named after the fictional "Tom Jones" from the book: "The History of Tom Jones, a Foundling".
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     The plot includes rowdiness, drunkiness, swordfights, lies, schemes, wanton females (and males) and a great deal of humour.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     Which is to say it has lots of things going for it. Part comedy, part soap opera, part three-musketeers-style duels.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     In other words it is really entertaining television. In its original book format it included an handful of moral and ethical dilemnas that forced Henry Fielding's contemporaries to think hard, ideas that by today's standards of marrying for love, honesty in a relationship, fidelity and so forth - doesn't seem so unorthodox these days, but instead just helps to make a great comedy / drama.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     And you can watch all of it for free on YouTube. :)
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     <center>
                      <iframe allowfullscreen="" frameborder="0" height="413" src="//www.youtube.com/embed/YMQAJA56gX0?rel=0" width="550">
                      </iframe>
                      <br/>
                      <br/>
                      <iframe allowfullscreen="" frameborder="0" height="413" src="//www.youtube.com/embed/Bh6kafArhW0?rel=0" width="550">
                      </iframe>
                      <br/>
                     </center>

                     </div>
