                 <h2 class="date-header">
                  <span>
                   Wednesday, July 10, 2013
                  </span>
                 </h2>
                 <div class="date-posts">
                  <div class="post-outer">
                   <div class="post hentry">
                    <a name="551362442281520759">
                    </a>
                    <h3 class="post-title entry-title">
                     <a href="http://www.productreviewscanada.com/2013/07/deep-space-nine-review.html">
                      Deep Space Nine Review
                     </a>
                    </h3>
                    <div class="post-header">
                     <div class="post-header-line-1">
                      <div class="post-share-buttons goog-inline-block">
                       <a class="goog-inline-block share-button sb-email" href="https://www.blogger.com/share-post.g?blogID=801925266976884095&amp;postID=551362442281520759&amp;target=email" target="_blank" title="Email This">
                        <span class="share-button-link-text">
                         Email This
                        </span>
                       </a>
                       <a class="goog-inline-block share-button sb-blog" href="https://www.blogger.com/share-post.g?blogID=801925266976884095&amp;postID=551362442281520759&amp;target=blog" onclick='window.open(this.href, "_blank", "height=270,width=475"); return false;' target="_blank" title="BlogThis!">
                        <span class="share-button-link-text">
                         BlogThis!
                        </span>
                       </a>
                       <a class="goog-inline-block share-button sb-twitter" href="https://www.blogger.com/share-post.g?blogID=801925266976884095&amp;postID=551362442281520759&amp;target=twitter" target="_blank" title="Share to Twitter">
                        <span class="share-button-link-text">
                         Share to Twitter
                        </span>
                       </a>
                       <a class="goog-inline-block share-button sb-facebook" href="https://www.blogger.com/share-post.g?blogID=801925266976884095&amp;postID=551362442281520759&amp;target=facebook" onclick='window.open(this.href, "_blank", "height=430,width=640"); return false;' target="_blank" title="Share to Facebook">
                        <span class="share-button-link-text">
                         Share to Facebook
                        </span>
                       </a>
                       <a class="goog-inline-block share-button sb-pinterest" href="https://www.blogger.com/share-post.g?blogID=801925266976884095&amp;postID=551362442281520759&amp;target=pinterest" target="_blank" title="Share to Pinterest">
                        <span class="share-button-link-text">
                         Share to Pinterest
                        </span>
                       </a>
                       <div class="goog-inline-block dummy-container">
                        <g:plusone annotation="inline" href="http://www.productreviewscanada.com/2013/07/deep-space-nine-review.html" size="medium" source="blogger:blog:plusone" width="300">
                        </g:plusone>
                       </div>
                      </div>
                      <span class="post-timestamp">
                       at
                       <a class="timestamp-link" href="http://www.productreviewscanada.com/2013/07/deep-space-nine-review.html" rel="bookmark" title="permanent link">
                        <abbr class="published" title="2013-07-10T16:48:00-07:00">
                         4:48 PM
                        </abbr>
                       </a>
                      </span>
                     </div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="post-body entry-content" id="post-body-551362442281520759">
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-L9tjXz6MWi8/Ud3usq8CwgI/AAAAAAAAVa4/gBzJ_DZvlro/s1600/Deep+Space+Nine+Review.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="clear: right; float: right; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 1em;">
                       <img border="0" height="300" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-L9tjXz6MWi8/Ud3usq8CwgI/AAAAAAAAVa4/gBzJ_DZvlro/s400/Deep+Space+Nine+Review.jpg" width="400"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     I am currently in the final stages of watching ALL of the
                     <b>
                      Deep Space Nine (Star Trek)
                     </b>
                     episodes.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     Now to be fair, I used to hate Deep Space Nine. The show to me was a bit of a dud. I thought it was too much like a soap opera, I didn't really like the characters (especially Quark who I found super annoying), and I didn't really give the show a fair chance.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     But now, after watching 6 and a half seasons of it, and I will likely finish season 7 in the next 4 days, I must admit I really was treating the show unfairly. Again, I blame Quark.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     However now that I have seen (almost) all of it Quark and many of the other characters have grown on me. The show I used to hate and make fun of (mostly due to my own refusal to watch it unless I had to) has now proven itself worthy.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     Basically it all comes down to the fact that I realized about a month ago that I had never given the show a fair chance and decided to watch season 1 to see if I liked it. Turns out I did. Six and a half seasons later I am very happy I gave the show a chance.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-7qHzmZe85JM/Ud3useOCgyI/AAAAAAAAVa0/Tvxw7F8C1hg/s1600/Gagh-Klingon-Food.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="clear: right; float: right; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 1em;">
                       <img border="0" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-7qHzmZe85JM/Ud3useOCgyI/AAAAAAAAVa0/Tvxw7F8C1hg/s1600/Gagh-Klingon-Food.jpg"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     It is a bit like trying a new food that looks a bit disgusting - like the Klingon dish "gagh" (pronunced "gack"), which is basically live squirming worms. Yes, you don't like it because it visually looks unappealing, slimy and disgusting - but for all I know it could be very tasty and amazing. No idea. It is after all a fictional food.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     But now, after trying it, I must admit Deep Space Nine was far better than I was expecting - and well worthy of the Star Trek name.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     I also thoroughly enjoy all of the original series of Star Trek, most of the Next Generation episodes, most of Voyager episodes and most of the Enterprise episodes.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     Despite what some people think I also think Enterprise was a fine show and that it wasn't due to any lack of quality that the show's ratings suffered. The problem was that audiences had become a little too fed up on "too much Star Trek". The tv shows, the movies, Star Trek conventions, science fiction TV shows that are basically a rip off from Star Trek... shows like Babylon 5, Battlestar Gallactica, Farscape, Andromeda, Firefly, etc...
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     Now I realize that some fans out there will get upset that their favourite show is being accused of being a "rip off" of Star Trek, so let me explain. Star Trek was basically the first space trekking TV show about a spaceship. Everything that comes after that - regardless of plot, ship design, etc - is essentially a rip off, even if they are deliberately trying to avoid that connection.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     Star Trek is essentially the alpha and omega when it comes to science fiction TV shows about spaceships. There are other sources of science fiction (mostly books) that came before that, but Star Trek is the "big man on campus".
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     And for those people out there who want to pipe up and mention Star Wars, I must remind you that
                     <b>
                      Star Wars is not science fiction
                     </b>
                     - it is a fantasy adventure story (and episodes I, II and III all rather suck). Star Wars has magic (the force), light sabres (swords) and floating castles in space (death stars) and swashbuckling rogues with names like Han Solo. Take away the space travel and replace it with sailing ships and it is more like Pirates of the Caribbean than anything else.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     Yada yada yada, I think I have made my point. Deep Space Nine is good.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     Various other science fiction TV shows are also good. Sometimes.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     Episodes I, II and III of Star Wars all suck.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     Oh! And Star Trek V - The Final Frontier, worst Star Trek movie ever. Star Trek II - The Wrath of Khan and Star Trek IV - The Voyage Home are awesome! :)
                     <br/>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                     </div>
                     <div style="clear: both;">
                     </div>
                    </div>

                    <h3 class="post-title entry-title">
                     <a href="http://www.productreviewscanada.com/2013/02/oscar-party-life-of-pi.html">
                      Oscar party: The Life of Pi
                     </a>
                    </h3>
                    <div class="post-header">
                     <div class="post-header-line-1">
                      <div class="post-share-buttons goog-inline-block">
                       <a class="goog-inline-block share-button sb-email" href="https://www.blogger.com/share-post.g?blogID=801925266976884095&amp;postID=2665425928551184924&amp;target=email" target="_blank" title="Email This">
                        <span class="share-button-link-text">
                         Email This
                        </span>
                       </a>
                       <a class="goog-inline-block share-button sb-blog" href="https://www.blogger.com/share-post.g?blogID=801925266976884095&amp;postID=2665425928551184924&amp;target=blog" onclick='window.open(this.href, "_blank", "height=270,width=475"); return false;' target="_blank" title="BlogThis!">
                        <span class="share-button-link-text">
                         BlogThis!
                        </span>
                       </a>
                       <a class="goog-inline-block share-button sb-twitter" href="https://www.blogger.com/share-post.g?blogID=801925266976884095&amp;postID=2665425928551184924&amp;target=twitter" target="_blank" title="Share to Twitter">
                        <span class="share-button-link-text">
                         Share to Twitter
                        </span>
                       </a>
                       <a class="goog-inline-block share-button sb-facebook" href="https://www.blogger.com/share-post.g?blogID=801925266976884095&amp;postID=2665425928551184924&amp;target=facebook" onclick='window.open(this.href, "_blank", "height=430,width=640"); return false;' target="_blank" title="Share to Facebook">
                        <span class="share-button-link-text">
                         Share to Facebook
                        </span>
                       </a>
                       <a class="goog-inline-block share-button sb-pinterest" href="https://www.blogger.com/share-post.g?blogID=801925266976884095&amp;postID=2665425928551184924&amp;target=pinterest" target="_blank" title="Share to Pinterest">
                        <span class="share-button-link-text">
                         Share to Pinterest
                        </span>
                       </a>
                       <div class="goog-inline-block dummy-container">
                        <g:plusone annotation="inline" href="http://www.productreviewscanada.com/2013/02/oscar-party-life-of-pi.html" size="medium" source="blogger:blog:plusone" width="300">
                        </g:plusone>
                       </div>
                      </div>
                      <span class="post-timestamp">
                       at
                       <a class="timestamp-link" href="http://www.productreviewscanada.com/2013/02/oscar-party-life-of-pi.html" rel="bookmark" title="permanent link">
                        <abbr class="published" title="2013-02-24T22:42:00-08:00">
                         10:42 PM
                        </abbr>
                       </a>
                      </span>
                     </div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="post-body entry-content" id="post-body-2665425928551184924">
                     <p>
                      I just came home from up really late night Oscar Party - and I think it's time for me to watch the movie The Life of Pi. I saw the trailer previously and I did wanna see it sometime but I just haven't got around to it yet. I am now watching it right now. Literally right now. Details to come later on how much I liked it or whether I hated it.
                     </p>

                     </div>

                    </a>
                    <h3 class="post-title entry-title">
                     <a href="http://www.productreviewscanada.com/2013/02/the-harry-potter-film-franchise.html">
                      The Harry Potter film franchise
                     </a>
                    </h3>
                    <div class="post-header">
                     <div class="post-header-line-1">
                      <div class="post-share-buttons goog-inline-block">
                       <a class="goog-inline-block share-button sb-email" href="https://www.blogger.com/share-post.g?blogID=801925266976884095&amp;postID=3022994159779273475&amp;target=email" target="_blank" title="Email This">

                       <a class="goog-inline-block share-button sb-pinterest" href="https://www.blogger.com/share-post.g?blogID=801925266976884095&amp;postID=3022994159779273475&amp;target=pinterest" target="_blank" title="Share to Pinterest">

                        <g:plusone annotation="inline" href="http://www.productreviewscanada.com/2013/02/the-harry-potter-film-franchise.html" size="medium" source="blogger:blog:plusone" width="300">
                        </g:plusone>
                       </div>
                      </div>
                      <span class="post-timestamp">
                       at
                       <a class="timestamp-link" href="http://www.productreviewscanada.com/2013/02/the-harry-potter-film-franchise.html" rel="bookmark" title="permanent link">

                    <div class="post-body entry-content" id="post-body-3022994159779273475">
                     <p>
                      If you haven't seen the Harry Potter films yet you'd better hurry up and go to watch them before someone ruins the ending for you.
                     </p>
                     <p>
                      The films are very good and there's 8 of them. So you really have no excuse for not watching a piece of film history. And a piece of literary history too.
                     </p>
                     <p>
                      If you are 1 of those people who have been living in a cave recently and haven't seen the Harry Potter films then evidently there is something wrong with you. It's past time you've seen them. If you don't someone's grandmother is going to ruin it for you because their grandmother will have already seen it and you haven't.
                     </p>
                     <p>
                      If you're 1 of those people who think that there is nothing that Harry Potter has to offer for you, I'm sorry, pull your ignorant head out of the sand and go watch it already.
                     </p>
                     <div style="clear: both;">
                     </div>
                    </div>

                    <h3 class="post-title entry-title">
                     <a href="http://www.productreviewscanada.com/2013/02/into-white.html">
                      Into The White
                     </a>
                    </h3>
                    <div class="post-header">
                     <div class="post-header-line-1">
                      <div class="post-share-buttons goog-inline-block">
                       <a class="goog-inline-block share-button sb-email" href="https://www.blogger.com/share-post.g?blogID=801925266976884095&amp;postID=5217155072217576863&amp;target=email" target="_blank" title="Email This">

                       <a class="timestamp-link" href="http://www.productreviewscanada.com/2013/02/into-white.html" rel="bookmark" title="permanent link">

                    <div class="post-body entry-content" id="post-body-5217155072217576863">
                     "Into The White" is a 2012 film about two British Airmen and three German Luftwaffe who become trapped into the same Norwegian cabin and have to learn to cooperate in order to survive.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     It is actually a very good drama film - complete with guns, survival skills and political commentary.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     <center>
                      <iframe allowfullscreen="" frameborder="0" height="315" src="http://www.youtube.com/embed/r3FZNHumVCs" width="560">

                    <h3 class="post-title entry-title">
                     <a href="http://www.productreviewscanada.com/2013/02/iron-sky-trailer.html">
                      Iron Sky Trailer
                     </a>
                    </h3>
                    <div class="post-header">
                     <div class="post-header-line-1">
                      <div class="post-share-buttons goog-inline-block">
                       <a class="goog-inline-block share-button sb-email" href="https://www.blogger.com/share-post.g?blogID=801925266976884095&amp;postID=8795301085944321511&amp;target=email" target="_blank" title="Email This">
                        <span class="share-button-link-text">
                         Email This
                        </span>
                       </a>
                       <a class="goog-inline-block share-button sb-blog" href="https://www.blogger.com/share-post.g?blogID=801925266976884095&amp;postID=8795301085944321511&amp;target=blog" onclick='window.open(this.href, "_blank", "height=270,width=475"); return false;' target="_blank" title="BlogThis!">
                        <span class="share-button-link-text">
                         BlogThis!
                        </span>
                       </a>
                       <a class="goog-inline-block share-button sb-twitter" href="https://www.blogger.com/share-post.g?blogID=801925266976884095&amp;postID=8795301085944321511&amp;target=twitter" target="_blank" title="Share to Twitter">

                        </span>

                       <a class="goog-inline-block share-button sb-facebook" href="https://www.blogger.com/share-post.g?blogID=801925266976884095&amp;postID=8795301085944321511&amp;target=facebook" onclick='window.open(this.href, "_blank", "height=430,width=640"); return false;' target="_blank" title="Share to Facebook">
                        <span class="share-button-link-text">
                         Share to Facebook
                        </span>
                       </a>
                       <a class="goog-inline-block share-button sb-pinterest" href="https://www.blogger.com/share-post.g?blogID=801925266976884095&amp;postID=8795301085944321511&amp;target=pinterest" target="_blank" title="Share to Pinterest">
                        <span class="share-button-link-text">
                         Share to Pinterest
                        </span>
                       </a>
                       <div class="goog-inline-block dummy-container">
                        <g:plusone annotation="inline" href="http://www.productreviewscanada.com/2013/02/iron-sky-trailer.html" size="medium" source="blogger:blog:plusone" width="300">
                        </g:plusone>
                       </div>
                      </div>
                      <span class="post-timestamp">
                       at
                       <a class="timestamp-link" href="http://www.productreviewscanada.com/2013/02/iron-sky-trailer.html" rel="bookmark" title="permanent link">
                        <abbr class="published" title="2013-02-05T15:03:00-08:00">
                         3:03 PM
                        </abbr>
                       </a>
                      </span>
                     </div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="post-body entry-content" id="post-body-8795301085944321511">
                     "Iron Sky" is a 2012 comedy about Nazis from the Moon who have been waiting 70 years to come back to Earth for their revenge.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     The plot is based on the concept of a group of Nazis building a colony on the moon in 1945 and then remaining there with their outdated technology, waiting for the right time to strike.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     And like I said, its a comedy.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     In the same vein that Charlie Chaplin's "The Great Dictator" was a comedy.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     Having seen the film I give it 3 and half stars out of 5. The trailer is below. You can stream the full film on http://www.movie2k.to/index.php and doing a search for "Iron Sky".
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     <center>
                      <iframe allowfullscreen="" frameborder="0" height="309" src="http://www.youtube.com/embed/He_PWsJqsVY" width="550">
                      </iframe>
                     </center>

          window.followersIframe = gapi.iframes.getContext().openChild({

            messageHandlersFilter: gapi.iframes.CROSS_ORIGIN_IFRAMES_FILTER,

              },

                window.followersIframe.close();

              'open': function(url) {
                window.followersIframe.close();
                followersIframeOpen(url);
              }
            }
          });
        }
      });
